<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">laet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lataz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>late (not early)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's too <b>late</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'t <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>geworden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's gotten <b>late</b> already.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tardy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She always arrives <b>late</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> (200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lanc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*langaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_4">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>langer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">langst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>long
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lange</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b>long</b> day.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kort</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>tall
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lange</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>tall</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kort</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>long (time), lengthy, a long time
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> duurt <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It takes a long time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> langst</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>gespeeld</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Who played <b>longest</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***laten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> (108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lātan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*lātan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lētaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave, to cause to remain in the same position or state
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>lieten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>left</b> it like that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave, to allow to remain/continue to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>Laat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Just <b>leave</b> it lying there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let, to allow to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>lieten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>let</b> him go.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to, to make; <span class="use-with-mention">Creates a causative phrase.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>liet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> spullen <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> grond <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He dropped his stuff on the ground.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to may, to let; <span class="use-with-mention">forms a optative phrase.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>Laat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> licht <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Let</b> there be light.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to may, to let; <span class="use-with-mention">forms a cohortative phrase.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>Laten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> kuil graven.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>May</b> they dig a hole.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>Laten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> bioscoop <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Let</b>′s go to the cinema!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to not do, to refrain from

***lekker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> (370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lecker</i>, derived from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lekken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">likken</i>). Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lecker</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans">Afrikaans</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">lecker</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">läcker</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">lækker</i>. More at lick.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">lekkerder</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">lekkerst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Having a nice taste, tasty, delectable.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>, mam!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The dinner <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> tasty again today, mum!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Good, nice, pleasant in a more generic sense.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>Lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Nice weather!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">attributive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Hot, sexy, physically attractive.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a>'n <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ding.html>ding</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's such a hottie!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Hé, <b>lekkere</b> meid!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Hey, sexy girl!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Healthy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">well</span>, in good health.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuten.html>minuten</a> nadat <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> klas klaagde, <a href = vnd.unilang:beginnen.html>begon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> docent <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> voelen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A few minutes after the class complained, the teacher also began to feel un<b>well</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***leren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a> (453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lēren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***lopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a> (438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lôpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lōpan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*loupan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hlaupan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlaupaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, go fast on one's own legs
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>gelopen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>ran</b> to the city.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hardlopen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hollen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rennen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, cover distance, follow a track etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>gelopen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He did a lot of <b>running</b> there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hardlopen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hollen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rennen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk, go <i>somewhere</i> regardless of speed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>gelopen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>walked</b> to the city.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">stappen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">wandelen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk in general
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>gelopen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He did a lot of <b>walking</b> there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">stappen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">wandelen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch, to run <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to extend in space or through a range</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often of relatively elongated objects or constructs</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be open, current, activated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose liquid: drip, gush, leak
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lekken</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">druppen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms a continuous aspect. Although it carries an implication of walking, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> vague and not emphasized.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>loop</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <b>are</b> you doing there?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>In Flanders, the word usually means "to run", while in the Netherlands it usually means "to walk". An identical phrase will thus be interpreted differently depending on the area where the speaker comes from. In Netherlands, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">rennen</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the common word for <i>run</i>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">loope</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lopin</i> (perhaps cognate with French), presumably a diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>loop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">leap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="gender incomplete">?</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>loopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dry measure of content</li>
<li>An apparently larger <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> measure</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>loop</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i>Werkwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><i>(Noord-Nederlands)</i> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">ergatief</span> stappen, <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>, wandelen

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a> (503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lusaz</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> (102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mann-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">mans</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>mannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">manneke</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">manneken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></a>, human male, either adult or age-irrespective
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zee.</i>
<dl><dd><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Old_Man_and_the_Sea" class="extiw" title="w:en:The Old Man and the Sea">The Old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></b> and the Sea</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>husband, male spouse</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></i>. The unchanged form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used after numerals only; it refers to the size of a group rather than a number of individuals. For example: <i>In totaal verloren <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> 5000 <u><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></u> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> slag.</i> (“5000 <u>men</u> altogether lost their lives in that battle.”) The plural <i>mans</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dated, now mostly occurring in nautical contexts or in dialect.</li>
<li>Compound words with <i>-man</i> as their last component often take -<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lieden</i> or -<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lui</i> in the plural, rather than <i>-mannen</i>. For example: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">brandweerman</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">firefighter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> → <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">brandweerlieden</i> (alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">brandweerlui</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">brandweermannen</i>).</li>
<li>Various alternative diminutives exist, including <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">manneke</i> (used especially in Flanders) and the dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mannechie</i>.</li></ul>

***mee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a> (100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mede</i> with the frequent loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> (cf. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kou</i> vs. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">koude</i> ["cold"]; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">slee</i> vs. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">slede</i> ["sleigh"]). The forms <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></i> and <i>mede</i> were subsequently distributed to different senses.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">adverbial form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></i></span></span></li>
<li>along, together (i.e. with one)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***meer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> (82)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mēre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">meri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mari</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*móri</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>lake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sea

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mêer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mēr</i>. This form stood alongside the older <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mêe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maiz</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> (288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">meid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>girl <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially of a premature age</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> boek.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give the <b>girl</b> her book.</span></div></dd>

<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mijnheer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mijnhere</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> (25)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mit</i>, variant of *<i>midi</i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mede</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midi</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matją</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mett</i> (through Low German). <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> (36)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mīnaz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>belonging to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>: my
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>my</b> mine.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mina</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mēnis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ore, metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Some senses are borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">explosive device</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">mine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tunnel for sapping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">misscien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meschien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">maschien</i>, short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">(<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>) mach schien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(it) may happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">geschieden</i>.
</p>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">muoder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōdēr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*méh₂tēr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeders</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">gemoederen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moedertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a></b>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b>

***moeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> (86)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">muotan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōtaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mote</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">may, might</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be necessary, to be required</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to, must
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>has to</b> / He <b>must</b> go.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>Moest</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Did you <b>have to</b> work tonight?</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">verplicht <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> hoeven</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> should, be meant to, be supposed to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> gestolen.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> meant to</b> be here, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stolen. / It <b>should</b> be here, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stolen.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You really <b>should</b> not do that.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> wet <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> 1 januari in werking treden.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The new law <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> supposed to</b> come into force on 1 January.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to go, to need to go, must go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> supermarkt <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I still <b>need to go</b> to the supermarket today.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> hoeven</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to go to the toilet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I really <b>need to go</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The past tense <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a></i> can be used in the present. In Dutch, one can ask "<span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>Moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?</span>" which can mean both "<b>did</b> you have to work tonight?" and "<b>do</b> you have to work tonight?". This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">modaal werkwoord</span>: gedwongen <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a> (472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mugan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maganą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*magʰ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*megʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be allowed

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may, can, be allowed to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b>can</b> come after all.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may go, can go, to be allowed to go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> koud!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You <b>can</b>not <b>go</b> outside, it's far too cold!</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may have, can have

<dl><dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> 10 juli 2019 bereikt la <a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>belle</a> fille <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> racefiets zwoegend <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> top. <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> voorgangers <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> 17de eeuw <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> frisse duik <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> voorlopig volstaan gulzige slokken <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> bidon. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> bijrolletje in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> historie <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> La Planche <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoeg.html>genoeg</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooie.html>mooie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-De_helling_van_de_mooie_meisjes_knijpt_de_renner_de_keel_dicht_3-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-De_helling_van_de_mooie_meisjes_knijpt_de_renner_de_keel_dicht-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a> (196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">moy</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mōi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nice, pleasant, clean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mawjaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, washed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mewh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wash, wet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">moie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nice, sheen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">moi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pretty, good, nice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">mūten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wash the face</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and possibly to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mundus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, neat, elegant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">mundation</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a> (272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">morgan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*murganaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*Mr̥Hko</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blink, twinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">moarn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">morn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">morrow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">morgon</i>.

***na.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> (203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nāh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēhw</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>after</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></span><span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a cardinal number</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bar, except <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form ordinal numbers in relation to a superlative quality. The number that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 1 lower than in the English translation.</span>
<dl><dd><i>Brazilië <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> 8,5 miljoen vierkante kilometer <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>grootste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Zuid-Amerika <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>grootste</a></b> ter <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>With its 8.5 million square kilometers, Brazil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the largest country in South America and the <b>fifth largest</b> in the world.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i>Naast <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> toonladder <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> kenmerkend <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gegeven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> bepaalde tonen, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> speciale rol <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vadi <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> samvadi, respectievelijk: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> belangrijkste <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> belangrijkste</b> toon.</i>
<dl><dd>Next to [the fact] that the musical scale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a characteristic datum, there are also certain tones that have a special role, such as the vadi and the samvadi: respectively the most important and <i>second most important</i> tones.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nāh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēhwaz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>nader</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">naast</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The forms of the positive are obsolescent, particularly the inflected one. The comparative and superlative forms are functioning as independent adjectives to an increasing extent.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēhwiz</i>. Originally the comparative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in Modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>nader</a></i>. ***nee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a> (55)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">neen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nēn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">none, not one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ne</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">no</span>
<ul><li><b>1992</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._F._Th._van_der_Heijden" class="extiw" title="w:A. F. Th. van der Heijden">A. F. Th. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> der Heijden</a>, <i>Weerborstels</i>, Em. Querido's Uitgeverij, page 23:
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> stemming <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> in.
<dl><dd><b>No</b>, the atmosphere <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> great.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used to show disagreement or negation.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> vergist <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a>.</i>: No, you are mistaken.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> televisie <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a></i>: No, you may not watch television now.</dd></dl></li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a></i> has an alternative form, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">neen</i>. In Belgium, it functions as a stressed variant of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></i>. In the Netherlands, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an archaic, formal form in spoken language, but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> quite common in written language until recently.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i>Synoniemen</i></span></h5>
<ul><li>neen</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i>Verwante begrippen</i></span></h5>
<ul><li>ontkennen, ontkenning, <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>, nietes</li></ul>
</body>

***nemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a> (284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nēmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">neman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nemaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nem-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take, to take hold of, to grasp or grab</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take, to choose out of some options, to pick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take, to use a particular route or type of transport

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> (136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>nette</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*netti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*natją</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ned-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn, twist, knot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Nett</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Netz</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">nät</i>.

***niemand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>niemand</a> (174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nieman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nieman</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">n-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>niemand</a></strong> (<i>genitive</i> <b>niemands</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nobody, no one
