***niet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> (8)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">niwet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*niowiht</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">niewiht</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">never</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wiht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing, creature</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The former in turn derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiw-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiht-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally a pronoun meaning "not a thing", and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> used to reinforce a regular negation. The pronomial meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> lost in Middle Dutch. English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">not</i>, and its older forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">naught</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nought</i>, were formed in the same way, but "not" also lost its sense as a pronoun and became a negation adverb as in Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Not, no: <span class="use-with-mention">used to express negation.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>Niet</a></b> storen!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do <b>not</b> disturb!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>not</b> true.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*naudigaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">needy</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nötig</i>); synchronically analyzable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">nood</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">noch</i>, from <span annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">until now, still</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nuh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">now too</span><span annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">now</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren <ol><li>still, as before

***nou.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a> (96)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></i>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>now; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i></span></span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> it <b>now</b>?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>come on; <span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating a certain degree of urgency or impatience on behalf of the speaker.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>Ga</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:straks.html>Straks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><b>Come on</b> and get going! Or you'll be late!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>so, well; <span class="use-with-mention">when pressing someone</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vertel.html>vertel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>waarheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a>!</i></dd>
<dd><b>So</b> tell <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> the truth then!</dd></dl></li>
<li>well; <span class="use-with-mention">indicates a certain degree of doubt.</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeker.html>zeker</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>Well</b>, I'm not so sure about that.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>wow; <span class="use-with-mention">indicates amazement or surprise.</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> waait <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> hard <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><b>Wow</b>, it's still pretty windy!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nummer.html>nummer</a> (469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nommer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">nombre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">numerus</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>number used as a means of identification</li>

***omdat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> (145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>because
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> ziek <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not coming <b>because</b> he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sick.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word order <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> subject-object-verb after <i><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></i>. Synonyms, like want differ only by this.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">doordat</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">want</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voegwoord"><i>Voegwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></b>
</p>

***onder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> (253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">under</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*under</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">undar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unter</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>under, downwards</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (to) under (implying motion).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It went <b>under</b> the car just like that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ons.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> (73)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">uns</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uns</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unsiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>us (objective form of <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></b> heden <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> dagelijks brood.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Give <b>us</b> today our daily bread.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*unsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unseraz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></b>, <i>inflected form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>our <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neuter</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> heden <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></b> dagelijks brood.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give us <b>our</b> daily bread</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame" style="float: left; width: 65em">
<div class="NavHead" style="background: CCCCFF;">Dutch personal pronouns</div>
<div class="NavContent">

</div></div>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Only used with singular neuter nouns in dependent clauses; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in all other situations as an independent possessive as well as with male and female nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">unce</i> (1240), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">uncia</i> (a twelfth of a pound) probably via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">once</i>. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">onsen</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">onzen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">onsje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">metric ounce</span> (100 <span class="Latn" lang="en">grams</span>)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Prior to the law of 1820 that introduced the metric system in what then united both the Netherlands and Belgium a variety of measures ranging around ca 30 grams were known by this name. The law of 1820 attributed the name to the hectogram of 100 grams. In 1937 the IJkwet of the Netherlands officially abolished the term, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still commonly used.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hectogram</span></li></ul>

</li>
</ol></div>

***ooit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a> (250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oit</i>. The further etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not clear, as there are no parallels in other languages. Possibly a combination of Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*jit</i> (cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">jetzt</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġiet</i> gt; Modern English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yet</i>), although this leaves the initial <i>o-</i> unexplained.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>sometime (in the future)

<dl><dd>I will go around there <b>sometime in the future</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>ever

<dl><dd>have you <b>ever</b> played tennis?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>once (in the past)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a> miste <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> NK dammen in Utrecht <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> trein in <a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slaap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>gevallen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> enkele <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> Groningen <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Zwolle <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> gereden.</i>
<dl><dd>So <b>once</b> he missed the NK checkers [tournament] in Utrecht because he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> fallen asleep in the train and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> ridden a few times back and forth between Groningen and Zwolle.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***oorlog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a> (513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orloge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*urlage</i>. In this word, two Germanic words merged, both having the prefix <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ur-</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oor</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oer</i>, with the former kept in compounds like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oorzaak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause, driver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oorsprong</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">origin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the latter borrowed from German). The first word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uzlagą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fate, destiny</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laga-</i> related to modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">leggen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The second word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uzleugō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leug-</i> meaning “oath”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlogen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">war</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> (19)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">up</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*upp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> bal stuiterde <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The ball bounced <b>up</b> and down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> onto, up onto
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> kat klom gisteren <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> dak <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The cat climbed <b>onto</b> the roof yesterday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used in separative verbs meaning “to go away” with rude connotations.</span></li></ol>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Naast <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> toonladder <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> kenmerkend <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gegeven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> bepaalde tonen, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> speciale rol <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vadi <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> samvadi, respectievelijk: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> belangrijkste <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></b> belangrijkste toon.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Next to [the fact] that the musical scale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a characteristic datum, there are also certain tones that have a special role, such as the vadi and the samvadi: respectively the most important and <b>second</b> most important tones.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Brazilië <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> 8,5 miljoen vierkante kilometer <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>grootste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Zuid-Amerika <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>grootste</a> ter <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">With its 8.5 million square kilometers, Brazil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the largest country in South America and the <b>fifth</b> largest in the world.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i>Bijwoord</i></span></h4>

</p>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> bijwoordelijke vorm <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> voorzetsel <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> dezelfde betekenisssen:</dd></dl>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">out</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">alt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aldaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*altós</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eltós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂el-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grow, nourish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">alt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">âld</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">old</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">old</i>.

***over.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> (62)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ōver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ovar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uber</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upér</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upo</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ober</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></a>, above</li>

***pas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a> (327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>passen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>passen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i>. Equivalent to a derivation from etymology 2.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_4">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>just</li>
<li>hardly</li>
<li>only, not until, not any sooner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>Pas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> opgeruimd, <a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> koekje.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Only</b> when your room has been cleared up, you'll get a cookie.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>now ... really
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Da's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></b> stoer!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Now</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>really</b> cool!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>fitting, having a proper fit, having the correct size and shape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> schoenen <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Those shoes do not <b>fit well</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>passen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pace, step; also as a measure of distance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mountain pass</li>
<li>fit of an object, notably depending on forms and/or dimensions</li></ol>

***pijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a> (382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">poena</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">punishment, strife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ποινή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poinḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bloodmoney, weregild, fine, price paid, penalty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>physical pain, ache</li>
<li>psychological pain, hurt</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pīnus</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tree</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***plaats.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> (452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plāetse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">place</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaatsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaatsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">place</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">position</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A settlement; a town, city, village, hamlet or the like.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">place</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">location</span> in a text.</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Space</span>, especially free space (e.g. volume, area or storage space on a medium).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> extensie <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>neemt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></b> in beslag.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This extension takes up a lot of <b>space</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">square</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">plaza</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">paved open space of any size in a town or near a building</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">plein</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">farm</span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">boerderij</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">boerenplaats</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plecke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*plekka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mark, spot, place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*plakjō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spot, stain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a> (192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i>, further etymology unknown. Cognates are found only in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i>. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>prate</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">prattle</i> and the various Scandinavian verbs were borrowed from these two languages.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk</li></ol>

***precies.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a> (329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">precis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">precisus</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">praecīsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>preciezer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">meest <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">preciest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exact, precise</li>
<li>accurate, careful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pietje-precies</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">preciesheid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">precisie</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></strong>
</p>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsof.html>alsof</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">blijkbaar</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schijnbaar</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'t <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> feest - <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Lotto gewonnen ofzo?</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
